without the sound, the Video Speed+ creates a new video with your preferred speed, that contains both the video and the audio part of the initial video!\r\nThe app. supports editing of almost every known video format or codec that exists (.mp4, .mkv, .ogg, .webm, .flv, etc). \r\nFor every editing it produces a new video with the same codec and format as the initial one.\r\nFinally, it worth to say that the app supports 4 different templates/options when creating a new video: \r\n1.\t1.\tCreate a new video and apply your preferred speed to the whole or to a scene of your choice from the video\r\n2.\tCreate a new video that repeats a scene of your choice twice.
